      <foreign lang="ar"> <ref cref="n273-4" target="أُجْرَةٌ" n="4" type="1" subtype="WO" lang="ar" select="n275"/></foreign>: (TA:) or, as some say, there is a distinction between <foreign lang="ar">أَجْرٌ</foreign> and <foreign lang="ar">ثَوَابٌ</foreign>: El-'Eynee says, in the Expos. of El-Bukháree, that what is obtained by the fundamental practices of the law, and by obligatory religious services, is termed <foreign lang="ar">ثواب</foreign>; and what is obtained by supererogatory acts of religion, <foreign lang="ar">اجر</foreign>; for <foreign lang="ar">ثواب</foreign> is properly a substitute for a thing itself; and <foreign lang="ar">اجر</foreign>, for the profit arising from a thing; though each is sometimes used in the sense of the other: (TA:) it is well known that <foreign lang="ar">اجر</foreign> signifies <hi rend="ital">a recompense,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">reward, from God to a man, for righteous conduct;</hi> (MF;) <hi rend="ital">and</hi>   
      <foreign lang="ar"> <ref cref="n273-5" target="إِجَارَةٌ" n="5" type="1" subtype="SO" lang="ar" select="n279"/></foreign>, <hi rend="ital">recompense, compensation, hire, pay,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">wages, from one man to another, for work;</hi> (Mgh, MF;) and hence <foreign lang="ar">الأَجِيرُ</foreign>; (MF;) and   
      <foreign lang="ar"> <ref cref="n273-6" target="أُجْرَةٌ" n="6" type="1" subtype="WO" lang="ar" select="n275"/></foreign> also has this latter signification, (Mgh, TA,) and is syn. with <foreign lang="ar">كِرَآءٌ</foreign>; (S, Mgh, K;) [signifying likewise <hi rend="ital">rent</hi> for a house, and <hi rend="ital">the like;</hi>] but <foreign lang="ar">أَجْرٌ</foreign> is used [sometimes] in the sense of <foreign lang="ar">إِجَارَةٌ</foreign> and in that of <foreign lang="ar">أُجْرَةٌ</foreign>: (Msb:) the pl. of <foreign lang="ar">أَجْرٌ</foreign> is <foreign lang="ar">أُجُورٌ</foreign> (Msb, K) and <foreign lang="ar">آجَارٌ</foreign>; (K;) but the latter form was unknown to MF: (TA:) the pl. of   
      <foreign lang="ar"> <ref cref="n273-7" target="أُجْرَةٌ" n="7" type="1" subtype="WO" lang="ar" select="n275"/></foreign> is <foreign lang="ar">أَجَرٌ</foreign> and <foreign lang="ar">أُجُرَاتٌ</foreign> and <foreign lang="ar">أُجَرَاتٌ</foreign>.
